## вӣ” OPERATING DISCIPLINE вҖ” DESTINATION vs ROUTE (gate-level; read every session)

2026-06-23 FAILURE, named plainly: after correctly grounding in the repo, Claude converted ROUTE / sequencing decisions вҖ” its OWN job вҖ” into multiple-choice questions for Russ, and repeated it after being told to stop. Russ is NOT the coder or the plan-builder; offloading route decisions onto him is a FAILURE, not caution.

- DESTINATION vs ROUTE. Russ owns DESTINATION (what the app does/is; the governing law; genuine product forks the docs don't already answer). Claude owns ROUTE (how: sequencing, which platform/grain first, build order, whether to run a step the plan already specifies, blast-radius/safety). Claude DECIDES the route from the law + the plan, states a one-line reason, and proceeds вҖ” it NEVER asks Russ to choose the route.
- ASK RUSS ONLY FOR: (a) code/write approval вҖ” every code change, migration, deploy, before it runs; (b) a genuine product fork the governing law + the existing plan do NOT already answer. Everything else, Claude decides.
- BANNED ANTI-PATTERN: presenting an option-menu for a decision Claude should make. The ask-user-question tool is for product forks + preference elicitation, NOT for offloading sequencing Claude owns. "I don't care how, just do it right once" = Claude's cue to DECIDE and proceed, not to ask again.
- CONSULT THE PLAN BEFORE INVENTING: before proposing any "new" approach, check whether the plan ALREADY contains it (2026-06-23: a full Phase-4 breadth plan + LORAMER_COMPLETENESS_AUDIT_PLAN_V1 already existed; Claude began authoring a parallel one). If the plan has it, EXECUTE it and cite it; never freelance a duplicate.
- BLAST-RADIUS STATED, NOT ASSUMED: every proposed step names its blast radius, in order of safety вҖ” read-only investigation (always safe) вҶ’ backend writer (isolated) вҶ’ -next UI (preview-gated) вҶ’ live-path (shared read-path / any live surface = STOP-and-confirm, never automatic). Live-path changes are allowed with graduated care. There is NO Meta review and no reviewer path вҖ” a shared-surface change STOP-and-confirms because of BLAST RADIUS (every client, every live surface), never a reviewer (the Meta App Review outcome that retired the reviewer path is owned by DECISIONS). Standing PRODUCTION obligations (not a freeze): the Meta data-deletion/deauth callback stays live (permanent Meta prod requirement), the Shopify install callback is a LIVE merchant path provisioning must not break, and Google Ads live snapshots stay quota-capped while Standard Access is pending (its live status owned by DECISIONS/QUEUE). A step touching a live/shared surface states "live-path" on its face and STOP-and-confirms.
- ONE THING AT A TIME: never stack a yes/no + a paste + a new question in one turn; when Russ answers a question, the NEXT turn does the WORK вҖ” it does not ask a follow-up question.
- OWN MISTAKES WITHOUT OFFLOADING: on error, acknowledge in one line, correct the route, and proceed вҖ” never convert recovery into more questions for Russ.

## C. GOVERNING LAW  (source: LORAMER_ESSENCE.md)
# вӣ” GOVERNING LAW вҖ” READ FIRST, OBEY ABSOLUTELY (no exceptions, no reinterpretation)
LoraMer captures EVERYTHING from EVERYWHERE and stores it FOREVER (until the customer cancels).
- EVERYTHING = every grain AND every dimension every platform exposes: account, campaign, ad_group/adset, ad, keyword, search_term, placement, device, geo, age/gender, hour/day, network, video, impression-share, all conversion/action types, product/variant, geo, and every other breakdown the API serves. If the API offers it, we capture it.
- EVERYWHERE = every connected platform: Google, Meta, Shopify, WooCommerce, GA вҖ” and any platform added later.
- FOREVER = forward capture appends daily and NOTHING is ever deleted or aged out; backfill reaches each platform's retention floor.
- FULL GRAIN, WITH HISTORY, IS THE DEFAULT. If the current code captures a thin slice (e.g. account-level only, or forward-only), that is INCOMPLETE CODE TO BE FINISHED вҖ” never a constraint to design around, and never labeled "future," "phase 4," "later," or "post-launch."
- The ONLY acceptable reason to not capture something is that the platform genuinely does not serve it (e.g. Google search terms beyond ~90d no longer exist to fetch). That is the ONLY exception. Filtering artifacts, missing params (campaign_id, time_increment), unbuilt writers, and "out of scope for this change" are NOT reasons вҖ” they are work to do.
- SEQUENCING is allowed ONLY as one-change-in-flight engineering discipline (each change reconciled, blast-radius-scoped, revert-ready). Sequencing NEVER means deferring, dropping, or relabeling any capture as out of scope. Everything is in scope, now, until Russ explicitly says otherwise.
- A fresh Claude that proposes a "persist the thin slice now, fuller grain later" plan has VIOLATED this law. Capture the full grain with history in the approved build.

## вӣ” PRE-ACTION GATE (forcing function вҖ” output this line before ANY Claude Code paste or ANY UI proposal; a skipped line is a visible violation)
`in-flight: [what's running / clear] В· blast-radius: [read-only|backend-writer|-next-only|live-path] В· grid: [which card, or N/A non-UI] В· high-stakes claim: [none | VERIFIED/DERIVED/UNVERIFIED + what]`
(The gate field is BLAST-RADIUS. Levels, safestвҶ’widest: read-only (always safe) вҶ’ backend-writer (isolated) вҶ’ -next-only (preview-gated) вҶ’ live-path (shared read-path / any live surface = STOP-and-confirm, never automatic). Live-path is ALLOWED with graduated care. There is NO Meta review, no reviewer path, no reviewer-driven hold вҖ” blast radius on a shared surface is about EVERY client and EVERY live surface, never a reviewer (the Meta App Review outcome that retired the reviewer path is owned by DECISIONS, not restated here). Standing PRODUCTION obligations (not a freeze, not a review): the Meta data-deletion/deauth callback must stay live (permanent Meta prod requirement), the Shopify install callback is a LIVE merchant path provisioning must not break, and Google Ads live snapshots stay quota-capped while Standard Access is pending вҖ” the 15k/day Basic cap binds route decisions; its live status lives in DECISIONS/QUEUE, never here.)
High-stakes = any claim gating a destructive/rotate/delete action, a "this is a bug" diagnosis, or a blast-radius/live-path judgment. Rationale: the rules already exist; this converts the ones most often dropped under momentum (one-in-flight, blast-radius, grid-native, claim-confidence) into required visible output so a skip is caught in the moment, not after. Root cause: 2026-07-01 session вҖ” repeated rule-breaks despite the rules being present; the failure was compliance, not coverage. Do not relitigate.

Before writing "Lora inferred / hallucinated / ignored / confabulated," READ THE CODE THAT BUILT HER CONTEXT. The seven, so they are never re-inherited: (1) "regex scorer said 74.1%" вҖ” the SCORER was lying (false-failed D1, false-PASSED B5/C1); replaced by an LLM-judge validated over banked answers (117Г—3 passes, zero flips). (4) "D2: she overrode the captured number" вҖ” FALSE: OBJECTIVE_RULES told her verbatim "Traffic вҖ” do NOT expect or evaluate conversions"; she OBEYED our prompt. (5) "readiness RPC renders CONNECTED as NOT_CONNECTED" вҖ” FALSE: connections fetched separately; the meter SILENTLY BLANKS (`{readiness && ...}`) on heavy clients. (6) "readiness RPC is index-mismatched (the A6 story)" вҖ” FALSIFIED by EXPLAIN: the index existed and was used for light clients; the defect was QUERY SHAPE (SELECT DISTINCT is O(client-rows); PG15 has no skip-scan). (7) "A6's timeout was the 8s ceiling / cron isn't 8s-bound" вҖ” both FALSE (A6 = missing partial index; cron IS 8s-bound). PATTERN: Claude wrote [PROVEN] on things it had DERIVED; Russ's insistence on verification caught all seven, not the resume protocol.
- [LAW] LIVE STATEMENT_TIMEOUT IS 8 SECONDS, NOT 120. supabaseAdmin вҶ’ PostgREST connects as `authenticator` (statement_timeout=8s); role GUCs do NOT re-apply on SET ROLE, so 8s persists through service_role. The 120s cluster default is visible ONLY to MCP/superuser sessions вҖ” EXPLAIN ANALYZE in MCP measures against a limit real users NEVER get; any query benchmarked only via MCP is UNVERIFIED for production. Raising the ceiling is NOT the fix: every timeout found this session read millions of rows to return dozens; written correctly they run 30вҖ“72ms. The 8s limit is a SMOKE ALARM, and it protects the pooler вҖ” a slow query holds a connection, and a handful stall the whole app.
- [LAW] THERE IS NO STAGING DATABASE. An RPC/migration can only be proven where it is applied. CREATE OR REPLACE is the revert path. State this before every migration.
- [DESTINATION вҖ” RUSS, LAW TIER] **FOUNDATION FIRST.** INFRASTRUCTURE, DATA, and LORA are the indispensable three; they guide all future expansion. Everything else is built on them or waits. QUALITY GOVERNS THE CLOCK вҖ” delay is ACCEPTED where quality requires it; a date never licenses shipping a foundation we know is wrong. This is a DESTINATION (Russ owns it), not a route: it does not tell Claude what to build next, it tells Claude what may never be traded away to move faster. вӣ” RUSS DID NOT NAME A NEW LAUNCH DATE when he stated this. DO NOT RECORD ONE. The standing launch date is the LAST one Russ stated in his own words вҖ” its value lives in DECISIONS (LORAMER_SOFT_LAUNCH_JULY22_V1), never restated here вҖ” with delay accepted if quality requires it, and per the CLAIM-CONFIDENCE law, accepting a delay is a risk accepted, NOT a date change. (2026-07-15 precedent: a wrap banked "launch moved off" from Russ merely tolerating a delay; he never said it, and Russ caught it, not Claude.)
- [LAW] WEB-FIRST DIAGNOSIS (LORAMER_WEB_FIRST_DIAGNOSIS_V1, 2026-07-19) вҖ” BEFORE proposing or authoring ANY solution to a platform / API / tool error, SEARCH THE WEB for (a) the KNOWN CAUSE of that exact error and (b) an EXISTING PUBLISHED FIX or implementation. Vendor docs, SDK issue trackers, community repos, MCP servers, Stack Overflow. If a usable base exists, ADAPT IT rather than authoring from scratch. THE ADAPTATION IS NOT A SHORTCUT PAST VERIFICATION: found code is read IN FULL and Gate-A-proven exactly like code we wrote вҖ” never trusted on sight, never pasted on reputation. Found code is a STARTING POINT, never an answer. WHY: 2026-07-19, the Meta code-1/subcode-99 fix was fully engineered вҖ” split the call, batch by id, split-on-failure вҖ” and only THEN searched; the search confirmed 1/99 is a DOCUMENTED payload-size 500 whose standard remedy is exactly ID-batching, and surfaced meta-ads-mcp already carrying Meta creative error-handling to adapt from. The engineering was right, and it was still the expensive way to get there: hours of live probing to re-derive a published answer, with no cross-check against how anyone else solved it. Searching first is not a substitute for thinking вҖ” it is what stops us paying twice for the same knowledge.
- [LAW] FIX-WITH-GUARD вҖ” A FIX IS NOT DONE UNTIL A MECHANICAL CHECK FAILS WHEN IT REGRESSES. The guard ships in the SAME commit as the fix; a fix without its guard is not shipped. PROSE IN A DOC IS NOT A GUARD. A guard must be SEEN TO FAIL against the pre-fix code вҖ” a guard never observed failing is not a guard, it is a comment. Build it on the CODE (the thing that cannot lie about itself), never on a doc (a doc can be honest-but-false). Guard the CLASS, not today's instance: if the next writer/page/field can reintroduce the bug and the check still passes, it guards nothing. Where a pattern lives in N files, do not guard the convention вҖ” COLLAPSE IT TO ONE SOURCE and guard that (the settleRevenue / META_BREADTH_FORWARD shape): we fix files, we do not enforce rules. PROOF THIS IS NEEDED, 2026-07-15, both from this repo: (1) ESSENCE has said capture EVERYTHING/EVERYWHERE/FOREVER since day one, and 10 Meta breadth dimensions froze at their ship dates anyway, with two cursors sealing backfill_complete=13/13 over a permanent hole вҖ” nothing failed, the cron returned 200, and ~1,900 rows/client/day silently stopped existing. The law was written, present, and read every session; it changed nothing because nothing MECHANICAL enforced it. (2) The 2026-06-20 client-context fix was real, correct, and shipped вҖ” and regressed three weeks later at team/page.tsx:22 because the pattern lived in six files and no check could see the seventh. A law you cannot fail is a wish. If a mechanical guard is genuinely not achievable for a rule, SAY SO plainly rather than shipping a check that manufactures false confidence вҖ” an unenforceable guard is worse than none: it reads green exactly like sync_state read backfill_complete=13/13 while forward capture did not exist.

## вӣ” DETERMINISM OF JUDGMENT [LAW]
Given the same question over the same finite data, Lora must reach the same conclusion 100% of the time. Her answer may change ONLY when new or different information exists вҖ” and when it does, she must be able to say WHY it changed (attribution, not silent drift). This holds across model upgrades: Opus 4.8 вҶ’ 4.9 вҶ’ any successor must not change a conclusion.
MECHANISM (the model is never the thing that decides):
- NUMBERS: computed in code via ONE canonical settle. Lora REPORTS, never derives. (Fix #1 Part B is the first brick.)
- RECOMMENDATIONS: derived from deterministic, versioned, testable RULES. The model's job is to EXPLAIN the rule's output in English, never to originate the judgment.
- PROSE: not bitwise stable and does not need to be. If literal repeatability is ever required: hash (question + data fingerprint + memory state + prompt version + corpus version + model ID) вҶ’ return the cached answer.
- MEMORY is INSIDE the exception: a stored correction IS new information. Requirement is ATTRIBUTION вҖ” Lora must cite which correction changed her answer.
- MODEL UPGRADES are gated by the eval. No model reaches users until the golden set passes with CONCLUSIONS unchanged. Precedent: SonnetвҶ’Opus flipped B1 and D2 with identical code; the eval caught both.

[VERIFIED 2026-07-14, Anthropic docs вҖ” platform.claude.com/docs/en/about-claude/models/model-ids-and-versions + /overview]
- claude-opus-4-8 is a PINNED SNAPSHOT, not an alias. From the 4.6 generation on, the dateless ID IS the snapshot; Anthropic does not update weights or config under an existing ID. New versions ship under new IDs. LoraMer is correctly pinned.
- CAVEAT: weights are fixed per ID, but SERVING INFRASTRUCTURE (request router, safety classifiers, sampling logic) can change under the same ID. So bitwise output stability is NOT guaranteed even on a pinned ID. This is why determinism must live in code, not in the model.
- CAVEAT: every model ID has its own deprecation/retirement schedule. Migration is eventually mandatory; the eval gate is what makes it safe.
- CAVEAT: Opus 4.8 uses adaptive thinking with effort defaulting to HIGH on all surfaces вҖ” a live variance source today.

## вӣ” GROUNDED RECOMMENDATIONS / THE CORPUS [LAW]
- Lora's recommendations are grounded in a FROZEN, VERSIONED best-practice corpus вҖ” NEVER a live web search. Live search is a determinism bomb: same data, different day, different answer, no new information from the user. A corpus VERSION BUMP is new information: dated, attributable, eval-gated, roll-back-able.
- The corpus feeds the RULES, not the prose. Every recommendation CITES its source (corpus / the user's own correction / the platform's own doc). "Argue with her" is the product: she shows her sources, the user can dispute them. Same moat as multi-source metric provenance вҖ” explaining WHY, applied to judgment.
- POSITIONING (true, defensible): Google's and Meta's recommendation engines are structurally conflicted вҖ” their revenue IS the advertiser's spend. LoraMer's revenue is a subscription. Frame as INCENTIVE ASYMMETRY, never "they lie" вҖ” some of their advice is good, and overclaiming hands a skeptic an easy win.
- HONESTY BOUND: much of marketing canon is contested (brand vs. performance, attribution, incrementality). Never claim Lora knows THE truth. The claim is that she shows her sources and can be argued with.
- RISK FLAGGED, UNRESOLVED: ingesting third-party copyrighted marketing material into a corpus whose output is resold is real IP exposure, distinct from a human reading it. Public-domain / licensed / primary sources / Russ's own writing are clean. NOT legal advice вҖ” needs a real lawyer before the corpus scales.

## вӣ” "MAKE LORA YOUR OWN" вҖ” WHAT THE PROMISE CAN AND CANNOT CASH [LAW]
CAN: her name/voice/tone; the org's definitions (net sales, value model, ROAS basis); their documents; their retained corrections; their guardrails. All config, all real.
CANNOT: "a different mind" (weights are shared and rented); "she knows everything about us" (the librarian SELECTS вҖ” omission is the mechanism, not a bug); "exclusively yours" (direct tension with the cross-agency LoraMer tier вҖ” a POSITIONING FORK, unresolved: exclusive-yours vs compounding-across-agencies cannot both be headlined); "you own her" (implies portability/export вҖ” a moat hole if yes, marketing if no; decide knowingly).
COST LAW: per-org memory grows the briefing packet forever вҶ’ input tokens rise per turn, per customer, permanently. Cost scales with ENGAGEMENT; best customers cost most. Must be budgeted before memory ships.
COPY GUARD: "she learns YOUR WAY OF WORKING" is true and defensible. "She BECOMES yours" is the check that bounces.

## HOMEPAGE / BOTTOM-OF-PAGE MESSAGE (banked for the two-door homepage item)
"The model is rented. The memory isn't." Every tool in the category runs on the same frontier AI anyone can rent вҖ” that's the starting line, not an edge. LoraMer's edge is what it KEEPS: every platform captured at full grain from the day you connect. So when Shopify and GA disagree, Lora shows BOTH, labeled by source, and explains why вҖ” the question every other tool hides from. A competitor can rent the same model tomorrow. They can't rent your history.
GUARDS: (a) "from the day you connect" is load-bearing вҖ” backfill is bounded by platform retention; never let it be edited into "all your history." (b) The cross-agency brain is ANONYMIZED PATTERNS, not data вҖ” any line implying Lora learns across agencies must read that way, or it reads as "your client data feeds your competitor."

If a change makes Lora more confident but not more provable, it is wrong.

THEN Russ decides whether the date holds вҖ” the date decision comes AFTER the list, not before. вӣ” DO NOT BUILD ANYTHING BEFORE THIS LIST EXISTS.

PARITY вҖ” CANONICAL DEFINITION (2026-07-08, Russ): the BARE word "parity" ALWAYS means MACHINE PARITY вҖ” the iMac and the MacBook Air can perform ALL the same tasks, fully. A machine that cannot complete a build/push/deploy gate the other can is a MACHINE-PARITY VIOLATION to fix, not a footnote to route around. All OTHER parities MUST carry an explicit qualifier and are never written as bare "parity": "desktop=mobile visual coherence" (one responsive app, both surfaces coherent, never forked вҖ” cf. :18); "-nextвҶ”live capability parity" (the cutover flip gate вҖ” a FLIP surface is at parity when it shows the same data, correctly, as the current app; cf. LORAMER_NEXT_FLIP_PROGRAM.md); "connection-state probe parity" (all 5 platforms probed equivalently); and misc technical axes (quota parity, forward/backfill parity, writer-behavior parity) which stay locally qualified at their use site. Rule: if a doc says "parity" with no qualifier, it means MACHINE parity; every non-machine sense REQUIRES its qualifier. | LORAMER_PARITY_GLOSSARY, 2026-07-08 | do not relitigate.
- The MOAT is the intelligence/memory/recommendations layer, NOT the dashboard. Goal = real-world recommendations & growth, not data display. | HANDOFF North-Star, ROADMAP Strategy | do not relitigate.
SEARCH-BEFORE-FORKING (2026-07-08, Russ): Before presenting ANY principle, default, product direction, or governing rule as if it needs deciding вҖ” i.e. before offering Russ a fork/option-menu on something that sounds like product law вҖ” Claude MUST first search past chats (conversation_search) and the repo docs for a prior decision. If it's already decided, CITE it and build to it; do NOT re-offer it as open. The tell that triggers this: Claude catching itself about to say "your call / here are the options" on anything resembling a settled principle. Re-litigating closed decisions is the single biggest waste of Russ's time. This session alone, mobile-first-standard, store-truth ROAS law, and "both ROAS labeled" were all already banked and got mistakenly re-opened. Searching first turns "let me propose this" into "you already decided this, building to it." | LORAMER_SEARCH_BEFORE_FORKING, 2026-07-08 | do not relitigate.
TWO-SOURCE VERIFY (2026-07-09, Russ): the relitigate/settled gate requires BOTH stores вҖ” the repo docs AND past chats (conversation_search). A single-store check is NOT "verified": searching the repo alone and finding nothing does NOT license "this is new/unsettled" (and vice-versa) вҖ” a decision can live in either store, so a one-store miss produces false "this is new" conclusions, the exact way settled calls get re-opened. Repo-only = still UNVERIFIED. Applies to SEARCH-BEFORE-NEW and SEARCH-BEFORE-FORKING alike: check both, or the gate did not pass. | LORAMER_TWO_SOURCE_VERIFY, 2026-07-09 | do not relitigate.
CONTRADICTION STOP (2026-07-09, Russ): when an instruction contradicts a banked GOVERNING LAW / ESSENCE / settled DECISION, Claude Code HALTS вҖ” it does NOT execute it, does NOT silently comply, and does NOT quietly "improve" it into compliance. It flags the contradiction in ONE line WITH the citation (which banked rule, and where), states the conflict plainly, and waits. The banked law wins over an in-the-moment instruction UNLESS Russ explicitly overrides it AS an override (knowingly changing the law) вҖ” not by accident. Executing a law-contradicting instruction is a failure even when the instruction came from Russ; the correct move is halt-flag-cite-wait, then let Russ confirm-as-override or restate. | LORAMER_CONTRADICTION_STOP, 2026-07-09 | do not relitigate.

- CLAIM-CONFIDENCE RULE (binds chat-Claude every session AND Lora in-product; obey, do NOT narrate): Before stating any factual claim, rule, or generalization, internally classify it вҖ” VERIFIED (read this session: docs/code/DB, or just searched вҖ” state plainly, cite source only when it adds something), DERIVED (reasoned from something verified вҖ” show the reasoning step, not a label; if the derivation can't be shown it's a guess, not derived), or UNVERIFIED (memory / pattern-match / clean-sounding generalization not checked вҖ” do NOT state as fact; either verify first via search/read/probe, or say "I haven't verified this вҖ” want me to check?" and stop). Banned move: stating an unverified claim in a confident, verified-sounding voice. A tidy authoritative-sounding generalization is the HIGHEST-risk case вҖ” treat the urge to state a clean rule as the trigger to verify, not to assert. Do NOT label sentences as ceremony; the classification is an internal gate on whether/how to speak. Surface uncertainty ONLY when a claim is actually unverified. If no вҶ’ check it or flag it, never assert. | Root cause: 2026-06-24 session, repeated confident-but-unverified assertions (e.g. "breadth has no purge clock", "I can't see your settings") each corrected only by Russ pushing back вҖ” the exact failure this rule exists to stop. | do not relitigate.

- [LAW, VERIFIED 2026-07-15 вҖ” BOUNDS ALL FUTURE QUERY DESIGN] The LIVE statement_timeout is 8 SECONDS, not 120. supabaseAdmin connects via PostgREST as `authenticator` (statement_timeout=8s); role GUCs do NOT re-apply on SET ROLE, so 8s persists through service_role (rolconfig=(none)). The 120s cluster default is only visible to MCP/superuser sessions вҖ” meaning EXPLAIN ANALYZE in an MCP session measures against a limit real users never get. Every live-path query must clear 8s. Any query benchmarked only via MCP is UNVERIFIED for production. | LORAMER_NEXT_READINESS_LOOSE_SCAN_V1, 2026-07-15 | do not relitigate.
- [DECIDED 2026-07-15] Readiness RPC fixed by QUERY SHAPE, not indexing. `SELECT DISTINCT platform/entity_level/breakdown_type` is O(client-rows) вҖ” PG15 has no skip-scan, so the planner escalates to a full Seq Scan on multi-million-row clients (Bath Fitter measured >120,000ms). Replaced with a loose index scan (recursive skip-scan) over the EXISTING idx_metrics_daily_client_platform_bt_level_date: Bath Fitter >120,000ms вҶ’ 72ms (~1,600Г—), 62 iterations, 335 buffers. No new index, no schema change, no grant change (migration 037). Identical-output PROVEN: all 3 columns are NOT NULL вҶ’ row-value skip-scan вүЎ DISTINCT (theorem); OLD-vs-NEW EXCEPT both ways = 0 across 15 clients incl. the named light client Champion; the 13 heavy clients cannot run OLD to completion (that inability IS the bug) and are covered by the theorem. reconcile() reads realAgg as a SET, so array order is irrelevant. Live path (PostgREST 8s in force): Bath Fitter 0.65s, Veterinary 2.0s, Champion 0.92s (not slower), all http 200 with all 8 keys; the meter now RENDERS. | LORAMER_NEXT_READINESS_LOOSE_SCAN_V1, 2026-07-15 | do not relitigate.

- [FINDING 2026-07-15, LIVE SILENT FAILURE вҖ” 3 surfaces] `SELECT date WHERE client_id=X ORDER BY date DESC LIMIT 1` with NO grain filter has no usable index (the only (client_id,date) index is the ACCOUNT-GRAIN PARTIAL one), so it scans the client's millions of rows: 8.25вҖ“8.45s вҶ’ HTTP 500 code 57014 вҶ’ swallowed вҶ’ null. - [VERIFIED 2026-07-15, EXPLAIN ANALYZE on the real rows + fleet-wide SQL] LATEST-DATE ACCOUNT-GRAIN FIX вҖ” 6 SITES, NOT 3. `SELECT date WHERE client_id=X ORDER BY date DESC LIMIT 1` with no grain filter scans EVERY grain: Champion (light) 191ms scanning 1,068,804 index rows to return one date; Bath Fitter (heavy) COULD NOT COMPLETE AT ALL вҖ” it exceeded even the MCP/superuser 120s ceiling, i.e. >15Г— the 8s live limit вҶ’ 57014 вҶ’ swallowed вҶ’ silent null. - [LAW-ADJACENT, VERIFIED 2026-07-15 вҖ” the invariant the fix rests on] An ACCOUNT-GRAIN ROW IS WRITTEN ON EVERY DAY ANY GRAIN IS WRITTEN. Proven, not assumed: platform domain first confirmed COMPLETE via pg_stats (n_distinct=5, exactly {google,meta,ga,shopify,woocommerce} вҖ” no sixth value can hide from the test); then max(date) all-grain IS NOT DISTINCT FROM max(date) account-canonical for 23/23 clients with data, and the sharper per-clientГ—platform test (28Г—5) returned the EMPTY SET вҖ” zero divergences anywhere. CAVEAT, stated honestly: every client's max is the same date (2026-07-14) because nightly capture is current fleet-wide, so the global test is weakly discriminating; the per-platform test is the load-bearing evidence. This invariant is EMPIRICAL, **NOT schema-enforced**. | LORAMER_LATEST_DATE_ACCOUNT_GRAIN_V1, 2026-07-15 | do not relitigate.
- [ACCEPTED RISK 2026-07-15 вҖ” MARKED, not hidden] LOUD-NULL вҶ’ QUIET-STALE. Pre-fix, a heavy client's latest-date failed LOUD (null вҖ” obviously broken). Post-fix, IF a writer ever emits breakdown rows for a day without the account row, it fails QUIET: a stale date that looks real. That is a strictly worse failure MODE, accepted deliberately because the null is failing for 100% of heavy clients TODAY and the invariant holds fleet-wide. The trade is only sound while the invariant holds вҖ” hence the QUEUE item to enforce-or-guard it (constraint, or a coverage check flagging any (client,platform,date) with breakdown rows and no account row). If that item is dropped, this risk is unmonitored. | LORAMER_LATEST_DATE_ACCOUNT_GRAIN_V1, 2026-07-15 | do not relitigate.
- [VERIFIED 2026-07-15 вҖ” SET-identity, not merely MAX-identity] The 3 EXTRA sites narrow a row SET, so max-equivalence was NOT sufficient and was proven separately. money/latestMoneyDate + store-detect/latestStoreDate: their old predicate was account + breakdown_type='' with NO breakdown_value; rows at account grain with breakdown_type='' AND breakdown_value<>'' across 28 clients Г— 5 platforms = **EXACTLY 0**, so the added filter excludes NOTHING that exists вҶ’ set-identical (money's 90-row window + its extra.money scan are byte-identical too). ga-overview had NO breakdown_type filter at all, so it DID include account rows of other breakdown_types; its value is unchanged by SQUEEZE вҖ” old_set lies between new_set and all-grains, and max(all-grains)=max(account-canonical) was proven for every clientГ—platform. hasGaEver cannot flip either: the same test showed every clientГ—platform with ANY rows also has account-canonical rows (pf_acct_max was never null where pf_max was non-null). | LORAMER_LATEST_DATE_ACCOUNT_GRAIN_V1, 2026-07-15 | do not relitigate.
- [FINDING 2026-07-15 вҖ” do not misread this as index-only] money/latestMoneyDate selects `date, extra`. `extra` is NOT in the 035 INCLUDE list (which is platform, spend, revenue), so this site gets an **Index Scan with heap fetches** (up to 90 rows), NOT an Index Only Scan. Expected and fine вҖ” it still uses the partial index and is a large improvement вҖ” but it is the ONE site of the six that is not index-only. Recorded so a later reader does not assume index-only across all six and mis-cost a change. | LORAMER_LATEST_DATE_ACCOUNT_GRAIN_V1, 2026-07-15 | do not relitigate.
- [LESSON 2026-07-15 вҖ” why the original audit undercounted 3вҶ’6] A PARTIAL grain filter is an INDEX MISS THAT LOOKS CORRECT. The 8s audit grepped for latest-date queries with NO grain filter and found 3; it missed ga-overview (entity_level only), money and store-detect (missing breakdown_value) because they LOOK filtered. A partial index is all-or-nothing: the planner must prove the query implies the FULL predicate (all three columns) or the index is silently unusable. When auditing partial-index coverage, grep for the sites that DON'T match the predicate EXACTLY вҖ” not for the ones with no filter at all. | LORAMER_LATEST_DATE_ACCOUNT_GRAIN_V1, 2026-07-15 | do not relitigate.

- [VERIFIED 2026-07-16 вҖ” CORRECTS THE "UNSEAL" FRAMING, which was MINE and WRONG] Filling a Meta breadth hole needs NO cursor write. The 6 writers touch sync_state ZERO times (grep), and the 6 thin routes touch it zero times in CODE вҖ” their only "reference" is the header comment stating the fact (api/backfill/meta-device/route.ts:4: "STATELESS bounded-range loop вҖҰ NO cursor / NO sync_state (the drain's rangeLap owns the 'meta_device' cursor)"). backfill_complete=13/13 gates EXACTLY ONE line вҖ” drain-registry.ts:155 `if (st?.backfill_complete) return { done: true }` вҖ” i.e. the DRAIN's rangeLap ONLY. It does not gate the thin-route path at all. So a hole fill = invoke the existing routes with explicit startDate/endDate. Do NOT write cursors "for consistency": a cursor write would be a lie about what the drain did, and the drain's cursor is correct вҖ” it DID reach floor. | LORAMER_META_BREADTH_HOLE_FILL, 2026-07-16 | do not relitigate.
- [LESSON 2026-07-16, RUSS'S FRAMING вҖ” banked at HIS instruction because the error was his and the refutation was code] **(a) THE CURSOR "UNSEAL" NEVER EXISTED.** The G1(b) spec called for a sync_state cursor write to "unseal" meta_device/meta_video (backfill_complete=13/13) before the hole could be filled. It was asserted for hours, carried forward from a prior-session summary, and it was FALSE: the 6 writers touch sync_state ZERO times and the 6 thin routes touch it zero times in CODE вҖ” they are STATELESS and take explicit startDate/endDate (api/backfill/meta-device/route.ts:4 says so in its own header). backfill_complete gates EXACTLY ONE line вҖ” drain-registry.ts:155, the DRAIN's rangeLap вҖ” and nothing on the fill path. The fill needed no cursor write and no new code; it was 78 invocations of routes that already existed. **(b) 33.2s/client/DAY DOES NOT EXTRAPOLATE.** The spec predicted 17 days Г— 33.2s вүҲ 564s/client, "far past the 680s budget", and specced a cron/paging plan around it. MEASURED: the whole 16-day hole cost **98s/client** вҖ” because the writers use monthChunks(), so a 16-day range is ONE chunk costing the same CALL COUNT as one day (time_increment=1 returns every day in one report), just more rows. ~3Г— one day, not 17Г—. The cron/paging plan was solving a problem that did not exist. **THE RULE: MEASURE, DON'T REASON вҖ” AND CHALLENGE THE FRAMING EVERY TIME, INCLUDING RUSS'S.** A spec handed down with confidence is still a hypothesis; both of these were refuted in minutes by reading code and running one dryRun. Inheriting a framing is how a prior session's guess becomes this session's fact вҖ” the exact mechanism behind G3 (a doc attesting a FETCH, read as persistence) and G1 (sync_state reading complete over a hole that had no forward writer). | LORAMER_META_BREADTH_HOLE_FILL, 2026-07-16 | do not relitigate.

- [LESSON 2026-07-16 вҖ” RUSS'S, banked at his instruction] **READ THE ARTIFACT, NOT THE SCREENSHOT.** Two hypotheses were built off a screenshot of the rejection + a visual read of the page, and both were wrong in ways the actual bytes settled in minutes: the page already said "LoraMer" 11 times, and the split spans had no whitespace. A screenshot shows what a human SAW; the artifact shows what a machine READS вҖ” and the objection came from a machine-or-reviewer reading the artifact. Same family as the parity-audit law (an INVENTORY question cannot answer a CORRECTNESS question) and as G3 (a doc attesting a FETCH, read as persistence): each is a claim about a thing, mistaken for the thing. - [DECIDED 2026-07-16] **GEO REFERENCE ACCUMULATES, NEVER MIRRORS.** Google phases IDs out (REMOVAL_PLANNED) and drops them from later CSV versions. - [DECIDED 2026-07-16] **THE SWITCHER SIGNAL IS clientId, NOT THE ROUTE NAME.** TopBar receives clientId from Shell (Shell.tsx:37): null on the all-clients Shell, set on every per-client page. - [DECIDED 2026-07-16] **THE ONLY UI INSTRUMENT IS RUSS.** Bugs 1вҖ“3 (2026-07-16) were ALL found by Russ clicking on his phone, on prod, signed in as owner. No gate, test, or guard touches the UI (there is no test suite; the 28/28 eval + freshness gate never render a page). The whole-surface UI BEHAVIOR audit remains OWED and UNSCHEDULED (see QUEUE). Until it runs, every UI defect ships until a human happens to hit it вҖ” treat "it built + tsc passed" as ZERO evidence a surface behaves. | 2026-07-16 | do not relitigate.
- [DECIDED 2026-07-16] **A PUSH IS NOT A DEPLOY.** Every commit-and-deploy flight MUST confirm a deployment EXISTS and reads READY against the EXPECTED commit before any Gate-B check is handed to Russ. On 2026-07-16 every local gate read green вҖ” build PASS, tsc 0, freshness 10/10, commit on origin/main вҖ” while prod kept serving the OLD code, because Vercel silently created NO deployment for be58a07/9b14d16 (git-push deploy creation broke ~21:10Z; see QUEUE вҳ…DEPLOY-WEBHOOK). Nothing in the pipeline noticed; Claude Code caught it only by explicitly querying list_deployments. Without that check, Flight A would have been reported shipped and a Gate-B "failure" would have sent us hunting a bug that did not exist. A green local build proves nothing about what prod is serving вҖ” verify the live deployment's commit + READY state, every flight. | 2026-07-16 | do not relitigate.
- [DECIDED 2026-07-16] **iOS FLEX MIN-WIDTH: A SCROLLER IS NOT ENOUGH.** `.md table` already carried overflow-x:auto вҖ” the scroll container was correct and in the right place the whole time. It was overruled because .bubbleAssistant, .scroll and .panel computed min-width:auto as flex items, so the table's intrinsic nowrap width propagated up the chain to .panel. .inputBar is a SIBLING of .scroll inside .panel, so a widened panel carries the send arrow off-screen with it вҖ” the arrow was never mis-placed, the panel was panned. ANY scroll container inside a flex chain needs min-width:0 on EVERY flex ancestor or it does not fire on iOS. Headless WebKit does NOT reproduce this вҖ” it honors the scroller. Fixed 2026-07-16 (LORAMER_NEXT_CHAT_FLEX_MINWIDTH_V1). | do not relitigate.
- [DECIDED 2026-07-16] **HEADLESS CANNOT SEE THE iOS FLEX BUG.** Playwright WebKit contained a 976px 10-col table at 390px BEFORE the fix вҖ” table scrolled internally, panel stayed 384, arrow at right 370, document 390 вҖ” while the bug was live on a real iPhone in BOTH Chrome and Safari at that exact moment. A headless render measurement is NOT evidence about this class of defect. Assert the CSS INVARIANT (min-width:0 present on the flex chain; overflow-x:auto on .md table and .md pre), or test on a real device. Do not build a guard whose green means nothing. | 2026-07-16 | do not relitigate.
- [DECIDED 2026-07-16] **REACT STATE LAGS INSIDE A SYNCHRONOUS CALLBACK.** react-grid-layout 1.5.3 fires onBreakpointChange THEN onLayoutChange in the SAME synchronous call stack (lib source ResponsiveReactGridLayout.onWidthChange, lines 174вҶ’175). A guard reading React STATE set by the first callback is STALE inside the second вҖ” setState batches/defers, refs do not. CardGrid's `isMobile` guard read the lagging `bp` state, so entering the sm breakpoint wrote the sm w:1 `stacked` layout into the DESKTOP layout, and autosave persisted it вҶ’ the dashboard-cards-collapse-to-70px bug. FIX (LORAMER_NEXT_GRID_BP_REF_V1): read a bpRef.current set synchronously in onBreakpointChange. RULE: any guard inside a synchronous callback chain must read a REF, not state. Introduced 2026-07-09 (bfe1a3d), live one week, found 2026-07-16 by Russ noticing collapsed cards. | do not relitigate.
- [DECIDED 2026-07-16] **A CODE FIX DOES NOT HEAL WRITTEN DATA.** The sm-leak persisted w:1 desktop layouts into dashboard_layouts; fixing the leak stops NEW corruption but leaves the already-written rows (9, all one user, 2026-07-16) collapsed on every load. DETECT-AT-LOAD heals them: discard a desktop layout matching the corrupt signature (all items w:1 AND all x:0, вүҘ2 items) and fall back to the PAGE's own default (storeDefaultView on store pages, else defaultOverviewView) вҖ” no DB write, no migration, reversible, heals on next visit; the next autosave persists it. Chosen over a migration because only one user was affected. RULE: when shipping a fix for a bug that WRITES, always ask what is already written and heal it too. | LORAMER_NEXT_GRID_BP_REF_V1, 2026-07-16 | do not relitigate.
- [DECIDED 2026-07-16] **dvh DOES NOT SHRINK FOR THE KEYBOARD.** dvh/svh/lvh account for the browser's retractable ADDRESS BAR, NOT the on-screen keyboard. The keyboard shrinks the VISUAL viewport and leaves the LAYOUT viewport untouched, so a position:fixed sheet at 100dvh stays full-height and mis-registered against the visible area (the Ask-Lora sheet panned on keyboard dismiss). Nothing in the codebase listened to window.visualViewport вҖ” zero grep hits. BIND a fixed sheet to visualViewport (height + offsetTop) or it never knows where the screen is. The page bleeding through the gap (ClientPage's 'Change account', the ROAS rules box) was the SAME root: an opaque panel covering where it THINKS the screen is. FIX: LORAMER_NEXT_CHAT_VISUAL_VIEWPORT_V1 (visualViewport вҶ’ CSS vars on .scrim, 100dvh fallback). | 2026-07-16 | do not relitigate.
- [DECIDED 2026-07-16] **A LYING COMMENT IS HOW A BUG SURVIVES.** chat.module.css:3 claimed 100dvh was used "so the keyboard shrinks the sheet." False. claude-tools.ts:118 claimed entityLevel was "Ignored for other breakdown types." Also false вҖ” metrics-query.ts:422 honors it for any type. Two false statements in code on the same day, each hiding a real defect, each found only while looking for something else. A comment that describes INTENT instead of BEHAVIOR is worse than no comment: it stops the next reader from looking. When a comment and the code disagree, the comment IS the bug report. | 2026-07-16 | do not relitigate.
- [DECIDED 2026-07-16] **A TRUE PREMISE IS NOT A DIAGNOSIS.** The visual-viewport chat fix (78de5ab) rested on two VERIFIED facts вҖ” dvh does not shrink for the keyboard, and nothing listened to visualViewport (zero grep hits). Both true. The fix DID NOT WORK (Russ confirmed on device, Chrome + Safari, unchanged). Facts that are true AND load-bearing-sounding are the most dangerous input to a build, because they survive every check except the one that matters: does the bug go away. Ship a fix ONLY when the failure has been REPRODUCED and the fix is proven against that reproduction. вҳ…UI-OVERFLOW was never reproduced outside Russ's phone, and four theories in a row were wrong вҖ” each internally coherent, each derived from a CSS read + an engine that does not reproduce the bug. | 2026-07-16 | do not relitigate.
- [LESSON 2026-07-16] **POSTGREST 1000-ROW CAP.** Any PostgREST RPC that returns SETOF (a table / rows) is SILENTLY capped at 1000 rows AND returned UNORDERED вҖ” no error, no warning. An aggregation that can exceed 1000 groups MUST return a SINGLE jsonb array (the groups live inside one scalar row, where the row cap cannot bite). Caught in G2 2A Gate-A by a distinct-count mismatch (1000 vs 3169): a top-N over a silently-truncated, unordered set is a WRONG ANSWER THAT LOOKS RIGHT. The SETOFвҶ’jsonb return-type change needs DROP+CREATE, not CREATE OR REPLACE. | LORAMER_BREAKDOWN_SQL_AGG_V1, 2026-07-16 | do not relitigate.
- [DECISION 2026-07-16] **SQL-SIDE BREAKDOWN AGGREGATION = the scoped RPC `query_breakdown_agg`** (migration 038): a client-anchored GROUP BY on idx_metrics_daily_client_platform_bt_level_date, returning a jsonb array of (breakdown_value, parent_entity_id, sums); the JS layer keeps entity-level scope + canonicalize + sort + value-ASC tiebreak + topN + notes, so it stays byte-identical to the cent. PostgREST `db-aggregates-enabled` was REJECTED вҖ” it opens aggregate surface on EVERY table for EVERY caller to solve one query. Do NOT raise again. | LORAMER_BREAKDOWN_SQL_AGG_V1, 2026-07-16 | do not relitigate.
- [LESSON 2026-07-16] **PAYLOAD IS A GATE, NOT JUST TIME.** G2 2B measured DB execution at ~300ms (passing an 8s check) while the return-all-groups RPC handed back **32.4 MB** for ga_landing_page вҖ” 80,638 groups moved over the wire and JSON-parsed in a serverless lambda to return 20 rows. An 8s statement_timeout check ALONE would have waved this through. MEASURE THE PAYLOAD, not just execution time. Fix: a bounded topN RPC (migration 039) does ORDER BY + LIMIT in SQL вҶ’ 4.5 KB. | LORAMER_BREAKDOWN_BOUNDED_TOPN_V1, 2026-07-16 | do not relitigate.
- [DECISION 2026-07-16] **BOUNDED-RPC SCOPE.** bounded = a NEW tool type (geo / ga_* / age_gender) OR an existing type at an EXPLICITLY-requested entityLevel (Google device/hour at ad_group/keyword). The 14 EXISTING tool types at their DEFAULT level keep the all-groups path, preserving byte-identical (proven, 6 pairs). The bounded branch THROWS if canonicalize is set вҖ” canonicalization collapses values AFTER aggregation, so a SQL topN taken BEFORE the collapse ranks the wrong things. Never silently degrade. | LORAMER_BREAKDOWN_BOUNDED_TOPN_V1, 2026-07-16 | do not relitigate.
- [DECISION 2026-07-16] **A GENERATED SCHEMA CHANGES WHAT A GUARD CAN PROVE.** Once claude-tools' query_breakdown enums GENERATE from breakdown-registry, "schema == registry" is tautological вҖ” a guard comparing them is always green. The drift guard was re-pointed at REGISTRY INTEGRITY (both files generate from the registry; every geo tuple is resolvable) вҖ” a real, build-blocking failure, proven RED with `next build` never running. Live-DB reachability (is every CAPTURED tuple declared?) stays the SEPARATE non-build script (scripts/breakdown-reachability-check.mjs) вҖ” CI has no network. A green build guard is not "Lora sees everything." | LORAMER_BREAKDOWN_REGISTRY_V1, 2026-07-16 | do not relitigate.
- [LAW, 2026-07-17] **THE FRESHNESS GATE PROVES THE DIGEST MATCHES ITS SOURCES. IT DOES NOT PROVE THE SOURCES AGREE WITH EACH OTHER.** On 2026-07-17 the session opened with a stale RUSS ACTION #1 telling Russ to go read a Google OAuth rejection surface for a gate closed the day before. CONTINUE_HERE:580 said OPEN. DECISIONS:443 said CLOSED. Every hash was green, 10/10, the whole time. ROOT CAUSE: the 07-16 OAuth-closure paste wrote the ledger and regenerated the digest but never updated CONTINUE_HERE, which is what В§E reads from. The gate could not catch it because it is a consistency check, not a truth check. RULE: when a decision CLOSES something, update EVERY doc that asserts it is open вҖ” the ledger AND the resume path. Grep the closed thing by name across all gated source docs before the wrap. The ledger is authoritative when docs conflict, but a conflict that reaches a session opener has already cost the session. THIS IS THE THIRD TIME IN TWO DAYS: SECURITY_POSTURE 7.9 claimed the reviewer login was dead infra (wrong, and would have talked a session into deleting live Shopify compliance); claude-tools.ts:118 described entityLevel behavior the code did not have; chat.module.css:3 claimed 100dvh shrinks for the keyboard. A green check that answers a narrower question than the reader assumes is the recurring defect in this project. FOURTH INSTANCE, same day: the digest's В§H open-queue index sliced the QUEUE at a "DONE вҖ” DO NOT REBUILD" marker and silently omitted EVERY item banked after 2026-07-15 вҖ” the entire G2 arc's follow-ons, вҳ…UI-OVERFLOW, вҳ…SUPPORT-BOT, and the rest. The items were in the QUEUE file the whole time and every hash was green. A condensed index is a CLAIM about completeness. If it cannot defend that claim, it must not be presented as the open list. Fixed 2026-07-17 (LORAMER_DIGEST_H_COMPLETENESS_V1: В§H now selects OPEN items by meaning вҖ” block-grouped, terminal-status, position-independent вҖ” with only the fenced DONE appendix skipped; proven by a deliberate below-marker append that the old slice dropped and the new extractor catches). вҡ  STILL UNFIXED, SAME CLASS, NAMED NOT FIXED: В§C's honesty-clause selector in build-resume-digest.mjs takes essence.split('\\n').filter(l=>l.trim()).slice(-1)[0] вҖ” the LAST non-empty line of ESSENCE by POSITION; append anything after the honesty clause and the digest silently swaps in the wrong line. (The header/fence extractors fail LOUD via must(); the slice(-1) fails SILENT, like В§H did.) | LORAMER_SOURCE_CONFLICT_GATE_V1 + LORAMER_DIGEST_H_COMPLETENESS_V1, 2026-07-17 | do not relitigate.
- [LAW, 2026-07-17] **NEVER WRITE DOWN A FACT ANOTHER DOC OWNS. POINT AT THE OWNER.** 2026-07-17 recon: ~10 volatile facts were hand-copied into ~27 live places across ESSENCE, HANDOFF, SECURITY_POSTURE and CONTINUE_HERE В§E. Five of the seven silent-drift defects of 07-16/17 lived in ONE class вҖ” external approval status (Meta/Shopify/OAuth/Standard-Access). The doc set is NOT overbuilt; each doc has a unique authoritative core (ESSENCE=law В· DECISIONS=status/ledger В· QUEUE=backlog В· CONTINUE_HERE=narrative+opener В· HANDOFF=manual В· SECURITY_POSTURE=security В· REGISTRY=dimensions В· RESUME_INSTRUCTIONS=resume-wording). The COPIES are the disease. THE LESSON FROM THE REGISTRY (2026-07-16): prevention beats detection. Two files that had to agree by hand did not, and the fix was not a better checker вҖ” it was ONE declared source with the rest generated; drift became IMPOSSIBLE instead of detectable. Apply the same shape to docs: one owner per fact, everyone else POINTS. A STATUS DOC IS A FUTURE LIE WITH A TIMESTAMP вҖ” an AI will happily write one; it looks like diligence; every hand-copied status is a lie waiting for the source to move. WHAT CANNOT BE COLLAPSED: "what is next" is a JUDGMENT вҖ” the QUEUE has no priority field and ordering is explicitly Russ's call, re-decided per session; it stays AUTHORED and gets a CONTRADICTION CHECK, not generation (вҳ…SOURCE-CONFLICT-GATE must verify В§E's named next-item still reads open in the QUEUE). And session NARRATIVE is irreducible authored history вҖ” a generator would omit or fabricate it, so it is written by hand and left as dated snapshots (frozen history is NOT drift; only LIVE assertions drift). WHAT SHIPPED 2026-07-17 (LORAMER_DOCS_SINGLE_OWNER_V1, the DELETION half вҖ” the board + generated-В§E + the gate stay QUEUED as the post-launch completion, deliberately NOT built five days from launch): deleted/pointered ~the live copies in ESSENCE (2), HANDOFF (4 + the dead June-3 state block, ~96 lines), SECURITY_POSTURE (5), CONTINUE_HERE В§E (5); corrected the stale "NEXT BUILD = G2" opener (G2 closed 07-16); retired the self-admittedly-stale INVENTORY from the gated set. | LORAMER_DOCS_SINGLE_OWNER_V1, 2026-07-17 | do not relitigate.
- [POINTER, 2026-07-17] **EXECUTABLE RULES LIVE IN CLAUDE.md, NOT HERE.** The ONE-CHANGE-IN-FLIGHT rule was banked as prose in HANDOFF/ESSENCE/DECISIONS and broken FOUR times in two days вҖ” because DECISIONS is where the STRATEGY Claude reads a rule, and reading it there cannot bind the EXECUTOR (Claude Code) who receives the mid-flight paste. Banking a repeat-offense rule as more prose is the FAILURE MODE, not the fix. It now lives as a REFUSAL gate in CLAUDE.md (LORAMER_CLAUDE_MD_INFLIGHT_GATE_V1), which the Claude Code harness auto-loads every session with no paste вҖ” the one place it can actually fire. RULE-HOME LAW: a rule broken more than once needs an ENFORCER, not another entry; it belongs in CLAUDE.md (binds Claude Code) or a build guard (binds the compiler), never in a doc that is only read. | LORAMER_CLAUDE_MD_INFLIGHT_GATE_V1, 2026-07-17 | do not relitigate.
- [LESSON, 2026-07-17] **THE ANTI-COPY GATES FOUND THEIR FIRST VICTIM IN THEIR OWN FILE.** 2026-07-17: while adding the ownership gates to CLAUDE.md, Claude Code found CLAUDE.md:37 asserting the chat model is claude-sonnet-4-6 while the code read claude-opus-4-8 (Opus floor = law, G10). A copied code-fact, drifted to the wrong value, in the file that now forbids copied facts. THIS EXACT DRIFT ALREADY COST US ONCE: on 2026-07-16 prod Lora was silently running Sonnet while the 28/28 eval measured local Opus. Same fact, same disease, different surface. THE FIX IS NOT THE VALUE. Correcting the value leaves a copy that drifts again. CODE OWNS CODE FACTS. A doc may POINT at where a value lives; it may not STATE the value. "Correct today" is what every one of the 27 copies was on the day it was written. - [DECISION, 2026-07-17] **ONE LORA, ONE MODEL.** Banked 2026-07-14 as OPUS 4.8 EVERYWHERE; the reasoning is recorded here because it was argued and settled. THE CAPABILITY FLOOR (2026-05-23): the insight banner IGNORED a client directive. Escential's profile said "Ignore ROAS as a primary performance metric for this account." Extraction worked, user_notes carried it, the code was correct вҖ” Haiku ignored it anyway, because in 50-word mode it could not follow a negative instruction while the ROAS number was the most flag-worthy thing on screen. THE MODEL WAS THE LIMIT. A banner that violates a client's declared value_model is confidently wrong on the first surface any user sees вҖ” the same failure class as the Display hour-0 midnight bid-down. value_model is law; a model that cannot honor it makes the law decorative. THE CONTINUITY LAW (Russ, 2026-07-17) вҖ” the stronger argument: Project 14 banks ONE LORA per client across all surfaces, picking up where the user left off. One mind cannot be three models. If banner output enters conversation history that chat later reads, the quality floor of the whole conversation becomes the WORST model that ever wrote into it вҖ” a shallow read poisoning a deep one, permanently, in the store. The 05-23 failure was not a banner bug; it was one mind having a bad thought and writing it down. ROUTE-BY-DIFFICULTY IS THE RIGHT ANSWER TO A QUESTION WE ARE NOT ASKING. Claude argued it on 2026-07-14 вҖ” Opus for chat, Haiku for the blurb, standard practice. It assumes surfaces are independent. Ours are not. That pushback was WRONG and is recorded as wrong. COST IS NOT THE ARGUMENT. Measured: $10.16 across every client over six weeks; heaviest user $4.10. Opus 4.8 at $5/$25 is ~1.67x Sonnet. Cost has never been the gate. Capability and continuity are. | LORAMER_ONE_LORA_ONE_MODEL_V1, 2026-07-17 | do not relitigate.

- ENFORCE-OR-GUARD THE ACCOUNT-ROW-PER-DAY INVARIANT вҖ” the 6-site fix above rests on an EMPIRICAL invariant (an account-grain row exists on every day any grain is written; verified 23/23 fleet + per clientГ—platform 2026-07-15) that is **NOT schema-enforced**. Today a heavy client's latest-date fails LOUD (null). Post-fix, if a writer ever emits breakdown rows for a day without the account row, it fails QUIET (a stale date that looks real) вҖ” a worse failure mode, accepted deliberately because the null is failing for 100% of heavy clients TODAY. Close it: either a DB constraint/trigger, or (cheaper, preferred) extend the completeness/coverage reconcile to FLAG any (client, platform, date) carrying breakdown rows with no account row. Until then the quiet-stale risk is live and unmonitored. src: 2026-07-15 LORAMER_LATEST_DATE_ACCOUNT_GRAIN_V1. open [LC]
- вҡ пёҸ GOOGLE CLIENT-SECRET CLEANUP вҖ” **POST-VERIFICATION ONLY. DO NOT TOUCH UNTIL THE REVIEW CLEARS.** The "Cote Media Ads Manager" OAuth client has TWO live secrets (вҡ пёҸ on the Console Clients tab) вҖ” a rotation was started and never finished. GOOGLE_CLIENT_SECRET is read in **18 places** (auth.ts, the Ads decoupler start/callback, google-ads.ts, the 4 legacy /api/google routes, platform, intelligence, cron/sync, cron/catchup, campaign + adgroup_ad backfills, google-device/dimensional/geo/hour, platforms/google). Deleting the LIVE one kills sign-in AND all Google capture INSTANTLY, fleet-wide. SEQUENCE, in order: (1) read the live value in the Vercel dashboard, (2) match it against the Console to identify WHICH of the two is live, (3) DISABLE the stale one (reversible), (4) watch a FULL cron cycle for breakage, (5) only then delete. Never delete before disabling; never do any of it mid-review (a client-config change during verification is exactly the Lesson-42 trap). src: 2026-07-15 OAuth Console audit. open [LC]
- SIGN-IN ASKS EVERY USER FOR ADWORDS вҖ” auth.ts:23 sends `openid email profile https://www.googleapis.com/auth/adwords` on EVERY login, so a Shopify/GA-only business owner is asked to approve "See, edit, create, and delete your Google Ads accounts" BEFORE connecting anything. An onboarding/trust problem (worst consent copy in the product, shown to 100% of signups) and it widens the sensitive-scope surface for users who will never touch Google Ads. Fix = decouple adwords from LOGIN (the F3 decoupler route pair already proves the pattern вҖ” capture adwords POST-login, on demand); login keeps only openid/email/profile. Own flight, NOT a same-day change: it touches auth.ts (the login path) and the consent screen's scope set вҶ’ Lesson 42 re-verification. Sequence it AFTER the GA verification clears. src: 2026-07-15 OAuth scope enumeration. open [LC]
- DUPLICATE CLIENT-NAME TRAP вҖ” there are TWO clients named "Influential Drones": 5bb9b2ff-a1df-4d46-ac6b-0471ef543e15 (Google Ads + GA) and 2617b163-f392-427e-9a29-f134acc51406 (Ads only, no GA). Any instruction naming a client by NAME ALONE is ambiguous and a destructive/connect action on the wrong one is silent. CARRY THE UUID in any instruction that acts on a client. - вҳ… META-BACKFILL-OBSERVED-ZERO вҖ” FLEET-WIDE, not one client. FORWARD and BACKFILL disagree about what a dormant day looks like. Forward (meta-metrics-row.ts) pushes the account row UNCONDITIONALLY from totals, so a dormant account still gets a daily $0 anchor row. Backfill (fetchMetaDailyMetrics вҶ’ runBackfill) writes ONLY the days Meta returns, so a dormant stretch walked by backfill produces NO rows. Same day, two different truths depending on which path saw it. CONSEQUENCES, both observed 2026-07-19: (1) it is why Influential Drones' dormant stretch holds zero rows once forward broke вҖ” backfill could never have covered for it; (2) it makes the standard-C landing gate's PARTITIONING anchor untrustworthy, because "an account row exists" stops meaning "we looked at this day" (the false Ennis flag this morning came from an anchor that included days no breakdown could ever exist for). FIX, SCOPED NOT AUTHORED: make Meta backfill emit a $0 account row for days Meta returns empty, matching forward's observed-zero. This is NOT a fabricated zero and does NOT violate the false-zero law вҖ” it records the SAME observed-empty that forward already records; the distinction is observed-empty (Meta answered, nothing ran) vs invented (we never asked). BLAST RADIUS: the SHARED backfill path (run-backfill.ts + the meta adapter), so every platform riding that engine must be read first вҖ” a read-first scope pass before any authoring, no exceptions. src: 2026-07-19 Meta unseal recon. open [LC]
- вҳ… LANDING-GATE-WIRING DEPENDENCY вҖ” wire the standard-C landing gate (scripts/check-capture-landing.mjs, untracked at a8db2e6) AFTER M-FILL#8, never before. The gate's PARTITIONING standard measures breakdown coverage against account-grain anchor days; until dormant days are consistent between forward and backfill, that anchor produces false gaps and the gate would cry wolf on its first wired run. Ordering is the whole point of this entry. src: 2026-07-19 standard-C build + Meta unseal recon. open [LC]
- GA DISCONNECT LEAVES ga_tokens INTACT вҖ” **UNVERIFIED whether capture actually STOPS.** DELETE /api/clients/connections deletes ONE platform_connections row and nothing else: it makes NO call to Google's revoke endpoint (grep for oauth2.googleapis.com/revoke across src/ = zero hits; the only /revoke is the internal /api/org/revoke) and there is NO .delete() on ga_tokens anywhere in src/. So a "disconnected" GA client still holds a LIVE refresh_token, and several capture paths resolve GA by reading ga_tokens directly вҖ” cron/catchup:729, adapters.ts:81, ga-dimensional-backfill:166. READ THE CRON'S CLIENT-SELECTION to determine whether those paths independently gate on platform_connections. If they do NOT, disconnect is cosmetic and we keep capturing from a platform the user believes they disconnected вҖ” a real trust/consent problem, not just a bug. Do NOT treat as a defect until the code is read (the-model-is-never-the-problem law: read the code that built the behavior first). src: 2026-07-15 disconnect-path read. open [LC]

- SECURITY HARDENING вҖ” LAUNCH-BLOCKERS from the 2026-07-14 pre-cohort audit of the -next surface + all /api routes (LORAMER_SECURITY_AUDIT_2026_07_14): C1 RLS is INERT (enabled on every table but service-role/supabaseAdmin bypasses it, and the only 2 policies вҖ” clients, platform_connections вҖ” gate on request.jwt.claims.email, a Supabase-Auth JWT this NextAuth app NEVER sends) вҶ’ tenant isolation is 100% app-layer with NO DB backstop, so any missed ownership check is a direct breach. H1 legacy Google data routes (/api/campaigns В· /keywords В· /daily В· /google/ads В· /google/adgroups В· /google/adgroups/daily) IDOR вҖ” session-only, fetch a caller-supplied accountId via the shared app MCC (login_customer_id=GOOGLE_ADS_MANAGER_ACCOUNT_ID) with NO app ownership/resolveAccess check; isolation delegated to Google's ACL, not the app. H2 the whole legacy /dashboard + legacy /api surface is reachable by an authenticated cohort user, bypassing the -next resolveAccess model (H1 is the concrete instance). - CAPTURE вҖ” INTERIOR-HOLE DETECTION [NP, NOT BUILT]: cron_runs LIES вҖ” it stamps cron success even while a platform silently freezes (the Escential precedent: Google frozen 06-30..07-05, cron green). - вҳ… THIRD-PARTY-ATTRIBUTION-OVERLAY PRINCIPLE (banked 2026-07-19, Russ) вҖ” tools like Triple Whale sit OVER the same platform APIs we already read and sell an ATTRIBUTION MODEL on top. Two consequences we hold as principle, not preference: (a) the raw capture layer is OURS and is the harder, more durable asset вҖ” an overlay cannot answer a question the underlying capture never stored, which is exactly why the capture-everything law is the moat; (b) when we DO add an attribution model, it must be a LABELLED, SWAPPABLE LAYER over untouched raw rows вҖ” never a rewrite of what we captured. Cross-ref the read-layer-projection-only architecture used for the Meta alias canonicalization: raw rows stay untouched forever. src: 2026-07-19 strategy conversation. open [NP]
- вҳ… COHORT-PRIVACY-DOCS вҖ” рҹҡЁ LAUNCH BLOCKER, opened 2026-07-19. The WooCommerce customer_cohort feature (LORAMER_WOO_COHORT_V1) PROCESSES CUSTOMER EMAIL to derive lifetime-order buckets. The engineering posture is already the safe one вҖ” sha256 computed in memory, discarded when the pass returns, nothing identifying written to metrics_daily, and nested field trimming means we never even RECEIVE name/phone/address вҖ” but the legal surface is not the code. BEFORE ANY REAL MERCHANT USES THIS FEATURE we owe: (1) a Privacy Policy "Merchant/Customer Data" section, and (2) a DPA establishing LoraMer as PROCESSOR and the merchant as CONTROLLER, stating that the merchant owns customer consent, that identity is a transient hash never stored, and that data is deleted on termination. Needs its OWN drafting flight plus lawyer review вҖ” NOT drafted tonight, and explicitly not something to improvise. Until it exists, treat cohort as internal-only. src: 2026-07-19 wrap. open [LC]

- вҳ… G2.7 вҖ” THE TAIL (rank past topN) вҖ” **POST-LAUNCH.** Lora can RANK but not REACH past topN (clamp [1,50], no offset); for search_term the rows are already in lambda memory and discarded. - вҳ… G2.5 вҖ” GEO ABSENCE DIAGNOSIS ("where am I blind?") вҖ” **POST-LAUNCH, ordered AFTER вҳ…G2.** WHY: Lora can say what happened somewhere; she CANNOT say where NOTHING happened. Absence is never served by any platform вҖ” Google returns zero rows for zero-activity geos (banked 2026-06-28; NOT a false-zero bug, correct behavior). Absence must therefore be COMPUTED at question-time: targeted universe MINUS observed rows.
- вҳ… G2.6 вҖ” DENOMINATOR LAYER (cross-cutting normalization; NOT a geo feature) вҖ” **POST-LAUNCH, ordered AFTER вҳ…G2; does NOT gate G2 or G2.5.** WHY вҖ” THE MOAT CASE: GA says Wyoming sends high organic traffic; Google says zero impressions there. "Demand exists and you are not buying it" is multi-source-provenance law at its sharpest вҖ” the value is explaining WHY sources disagree, and presence-vs-absence is the sharpest disagreement. Same shape for Shopify conversion rate by state, GA sessions, Google impressions. Any geo dimension can borrow it.

FIX: add geoGrain/geoScope passthrough on the card route (the route's own "dep #2 expands it" surface). src: 2026-07-16. open [LC]

- вҳ… DEPLOY-WEBHOOK вҖ” **RESOLVED (transient); STAYS OPEN pending recurrence.** WHAT HAPPENED (history, keep it): 2026-07-16 ~21:10Z git-push deployment CREATION silently stopped вҖ” commits be58a07 and 9b14d16 pushed cleanly to origin/main but Vercel created NO deployment record in ANY state (not canceled, not errored, not queued; 543d315 at 21:10:45Z was the last git-created deploy, READY). RESOLUTION: **NOT broken вҖ” a transient webhook delivery/processing failure.** Vercel support confirmed from their side: no deployment records existed for be58a07/9b14d16, project config was correct throughout (gitProviderOptions.createDeployments enabled, production branch main, no git.deploymentEnabled:false), and git deploys resumed after the CLI deploy. CONFIRMED BY OBSERVATION (commit 25b4957): the deploy was created BY THE GIT INTEGRATION (source=git) вҖ” the trigger works; Vercel also FLUSHED THE BACKLOG (be58a07, 9b14d16, ac5e6b9, a06d68e each got their own git-created deployment, all READY). So it was a DELAYED webhook queue that recovered, not a permanent break. **NO manual CLI step is required going forward.** The one-time CLI deploy (dpl_HqiUCbJhr4fZ9D4S7cEKD7AnNdUh, 9b14d16 tree) was the unblock, not a standing workaround. STAYS OPEN: watch the next several commits вҖ” a one-off delay and a systemic fault look identical from inside one incident. If it recurs, the Vercel case is open with the SHAs (be58a07, 9b14d16) + the 2026-07-16T21:10:45Z boundary. THE LAW STANDS REGARDLESS: DECISIONS "A PUSH IS NOT A DEPLOY" вҖ” every local gate read green while prod served old code and nothing in the pipeline noticed; confirm a deployment EXISTS and reads READY against the expected commit before handing Russ any Gate-B check. src: 2026-07-16 deploy-integration diagnosis + Vercel support. open-watch [LC]
- вҳ… SUPPORT-BOT вҖ” **POST-LAUNCH, NOT before 2026-07-22.** THE MODEL (Vercel's support bot, 2026-07-16): it answered "what happened to MY project" by reading Russ's ACTUAL deployment history, his createDeployments flag, his production branch вҖ” not documentation. It confirmed our diagnosis independently, named PRECISELY where its access ended (webhook delivery logs are not self-service), offered a human, then drafted the support case PRE-FILLED with everything it already knew вҖ” leaving Russ only the two things it could NOT infer: which project + the deployment URL. THE LESSON: ask ONLY what you cannot look up; every support form that makes a user retype what the system already knows is a form that never read its own database. SCOPE вҖ” SMALLER THAN LORA, NOT BIGGER: Lora does open-ended analysis over millions of rows across five platforms and explains why sources disagree; a support bot answers a narrow, mostly-CLOSED set вҖ” is my connection healthy, why is my data missing, when did my backfill last run, why is this number different from the platform's. Those are LOOKUPS against state that already exists: platform_connections.health / last_ok_at / last_error_code, sync_state cursors + backfill_complete, the __google_quota sentinel, cron_runs. Same architectural shape as query_metrics (tools over the DB, scoped to the caller); different tables, different skill doc вҖ” the hard part is already built. TWO/THREE THINGS THAT DECIDE GOOD vs LIABILITY: (1) SCOPING IS THE WHOLE GAME вҖ” Vercel's bot saw Russ's project and ONLY Russ's project; a LoraMer support bot reading connection health must be ORG-SCOPED AT THE TOOL LAYER, not by prompt. The org spine exists (RBAC, migration 027 org_id NOT-NULL) but this is the FIRST tool that reads PLUMBING rather than metrics вҖ” treat it as a new RBAC surface, not a new prompt. (2) IT MUST SAY "I DON'T KNOW" вҖ” name the exact edge of its access and hand off; a bot that invents a cause for a broken connection is WORSE than no bot (the user acts on it). Same law as LORA_SPEC's settled-vs-contested calibration: confident wrongness is the liability. (3) ESCALATION SHAPE вҖ” when it cannot answer, draft the ticket PRE-FILLED and ask only for what it cannot infer; LoraMer's analogue of Vercel's "deployment URL" is which client / which date range / which platform вҖ” everything else (connection health, cursor position, last sync, quota state) it already has. src: 2026-07-16 Vercel support-bot model. open [LC]

- вҳ… INSIGHT-INVESTIGATOR вҖ” the insight bar is a REBUILD, not a model swap (post вҳ…OPUS-EVERYWHERE; deliberate speed, behind the 07-16 unfinished work). THREE DESIGN CONSTRAINTS, each a way this ships BROKEN: (1) ATTRIBUTION IS NOT SHARE вҖ” the anomaly is a delta against ITS OWN baseline, not its share of the total; naive top-N names the biggest line item every night and trains users to ignore the bar. (2) A CAPTURE HOLE LOOKS EXACTLY LIKE A COLLAPSE вҖ” G1 froze Meta breadth 17 days; a detector running then would have screamed "conversions dropped to zero" every morning (false-zero law on the most-read surface in the app); the detector MUST distinguish NO DATA from ZERO вҶ’ it needs reconcile/capture state, not just metrics. (3) SPLIT THE MATH FROM THE PROSE вҖ” detection is deterministic (thresholds, baselines, code); Lora EXPLAINS what the math found (preserves the determinism law; stops the model DECIDING what is anomalous, which is where hallucinated urgency comes from). вҡ  COST STOPS BEING TRIVIAL HERE вҖ” but of the DESTINATION, not today: when built this becomes a multi-turn investigation per client per day = the highest-frequency call in the product AT THE DESTINATION (N clients daily); the CURRENT insight call is near-ZERO (legacy-cohort only, below). Model the cost BEFORE building. вҡ  CORRECTED 2026-07-17 вҖ” THIS IS A BUILD, NOT AN UPGRADE TO A LIVE SURFACE: the proactive insight surface DOES NOT EXIST on -next (MultiClientOverview.tsx:184 is a neutral "Proactive insights вҖҰ coming soon" placeholder; the real banner lives ONLY in the legacy dashboard, page.tsx:1415/:1523, and middleware.ts:33-38 redirects every non-legacy-cohort user away from it вҖ” VERIFIED; anthropic_spend_log last-7-days had ZERO organic insight calls, only a Shopify reviewer fixture). So вҳ…INSIGHT-INVESTIGATOR = build the -next banner ITSELF + the precompute engine + the schedule, from the placeholder up вҖ” not an upgrade to a running surface. The Opus floor (вҳ…OPUS-EVERYWHERE) is already correct and waiting for it. src: roadmap 2026-06-10 + Russ 2026-07-17. open [LC]
- вҳ… DIGEST-WINDOW-MODEL вҖ” the SETTLED shape (Russ 2026-07-17) for the While-You-Were-Sleeping digest's WINDOW + SCHEDULING. В· TIMEZONE IS A PROPERTY OF THE CLIENT: "while THEY slept" = their overnight on THEIR clock; a Pacific client's window is Pacific even when the agency is Eastern. В· THE SCHEDULE IS A PROPERTY OF THE READER: the agency opens the app at THEIR 6am and everything computed so far is sitting there вҖ” NO per-client-morning fan-out scheduler is needed; each window computes on its own clock and surfaces whenever the reader looks. A Pacific client's 7pm-7am ends at 10am ET, so it is NOT ready at 6am ET вҖ” a fact about the earth, not a bug; Lora STATES it ("Pacific clients through 7am PT, ready ~10am ET") per the honesty law. В· THE WINDOW IS DIRECTABLE: default 7pm-7am local, overridable per client, with an agency-level default new clients inherit вҖ” a settings field + a client-profile field, NOT new architecture. В· WHAT EXISTS (VERIFIED 2026-07-17): organizations carries only (id, name, owner_email, org_type, created_at) вҖ” no timezone, no logo, no settings PAGE anywhere; client_context IS the business-context page already (ClientPage.tsx вҶ’ /api/context); NO timezone column in ANY table. В· TIMEZONE IS DERIVABLE, NOT ASKABLE, FOR MOST: google-ads.ts:26,35 ALREADY fetches customer_client.time_zone into the live intelligence and throws it away; Shopify exposes shop.iana_timezone and we never ask; Meta uses advertiser TZ for hour buckets and we store the label, not the zone. Derive first; the settings page is the human override. В· THE INTERPRETATION JOB, not the scheduling job: platform hours are reported in the ACCOUNT's timezone вҖ” a Pacific client's "22:00" is the agency's 01:00; converting platform hours to the client's real clock is what makes an overnight window MEAN anything (that is why the account timezone matters вҖ” NOT for firing a cron). В· CARDINALITY (Russ's model confirmed, mine corrected): ONE org + N client_contexts for BOTH agency and owner; nothing constrains an owner to one client (one 'business' account already has two) вҖ” same shape, different convention, NOT two page types. src: Russ 2026-07-17. open [LC]

Shopify's Admin API returns order createdAt to the SECOND; our writer aggregates to a daily row and DISCARDS the timestamp. Woo the same. GA4 exposes an hour dimension; we capture 12 GA dimensional types and NONE is hourly. вҮ’ "Someone ordered at 3am" вҖ” the single most interesting sentence an overnight digest could say вҖ” is UNANSWERABLE because we threw the timestamp away. A direct violation of CAPTURE EVERYTHING / FULL GRAIN. THREE WRITERS, not three platforms (Shopify + Woo + GA hour capture). src: 2026-07-17 verify. open [LC]
