NOT via reports/coupons/totals (verified in the WC source: no date param, TYPE not CODE, counts definitions not redemptions, cached a year). coupon_type is an OPEN plugin-extensible set, not a 3-value enum.
    W-FILL#2  product category + tag grain (native Sales-by-category) [LC]  вң… SHIPPED 2026-07-19 (LORAMER_WOO_BATCH_WB_V1) вҖ” separate id-batched /products call; NON-ADDITIVE (measured 4.43Г— over net, up to 11 categories on one product); capture-time snapshot. product_tag ships and is honestly EMPTY on the probe store (0/71 tagged) вҖ” empty means the store does not tag, not a gap.
    W-FILL#3  geo (zero today vs Shopify's country/region) [LC]  вң… SHIPPED 2026-07-19 вҖ” geo_country/region/city, FLAG-NOT-BLOCK, BILLING basis (Woo shipping is empty for digital/pickup). PII: country/state/city only, never postcode/street/email/phone/name.
    W-FILL#4  customer new-vs-returning / cohorts (reports/customers) [LC]  вң… SHIPPED 2026-07-19 (LORAMER_WOO_COHORT_V1) вҖ” but NOT via reports/customers: /wc/v3/customers returns NO orders_count on an HPOS store (measured; the docs still list it). EMAIL identity instead (guests are 86% of orders, so registered-only would have been 86% UNKNOWN) вҶ’ UNKNOWN came out 0.00% and repeat customers are 55% of the real store's net.
    W-FILL#5  order-status dimension [LC]  вң… SHIPPED 2026-07-19 вҖ” ALL statuses incl. failed/cancelled/pending, which we already fetched and DISCARDED. WRITE-ONLY: all-statuses is a SUPERSET of the anchor, not a partition of it; extra.isSale marks the subset that ties to net.
    W-FILL#6  order time-of-day (writer discards timestamps; cross-ref вҳ…HOUR-GRAIN-CAPTURE-HOLE) [LC]  вң… SHIPPED 2026-07-19 вҖ” RAW, unbucketed. WOO-SPECIFIC: date_created carries NO offset, so the value is date_created_gmt normalised to UTC with both verbatim strings in extra; the row date stays the SITE-LOCAL day (re-keying to GMT would shift rows across midnight and break 7.5yr idempotency).
    W-FILL#7  payment + shipping method вҖ” вң… SHIPPED 2026-07-19. THEY DIVERGE: payment_method PARTITIONS (one gateway per order, FLAG-NOT-BLOCK); shipping_method does NOT, because shipping_lines is an ARRAY and a split shipment puts one order under several methods вҖ” so it carries the shipping CHARGE with revenue forced to 0, WRITE-ONLY. [LC]
    GA-FILL#1  ecommerce funnel steps (view_item / add_to_cart / begin_checkout + purchase-to-view rate + AOV + refunds) [LC]
    GA-FILL#2  Google-Ads-linkage dims (googleAdsCampaignName / network / query вҖ” the GA-vs-Google cross-check layer) [LC]
    GA-FILL#3  first-user acquisition scope (vs the session scope we have) [LC]
    GA-FILL#4  item category / brand / variant (we have name/id) [LC]
    GA-FILL#5  engagement / retention (bounce, avg session duration, active / returning / N-day actives) [LC]
    GA-FILL#6  full page-path perf (landing page only today) [LC]
- вҳ… CLAUDE-MD-COPIES вҖ” the copied code-facts enumerated 2026-07-17 (LORAMER_CLAUDE_MD_MODEL_POINTER_V1 already pointed the model IDs; these remain). FIX THE TWO ALREADY-WRONG FIRST: (a) the Supabase table LIST in CLAUDE.md asserts 9 tables and is missing 13+ that exist NOW (organizations, org_members, org_client_grants, known_floors, geo_target_constant, woo_connect_nonce, anthropic_spend_log, dashboard_layouts, user_profiles, uploaded_docs, sync_state, cron_runs, woocommerce_tokens) вҖ” a map of the database wrong by more than half, in the file the executor reads EVERY session; POINT at the schema (migrations/ + list_tables), do not list tables. (b) "dashboard/page.tsx вҖ” 3000+ lines" is understated (the file is ~4197); drop the number. The OTHER EIGHT are correct-today copies (same disease, lower velocity), each вҶ’ a pointer or dropped: 16k max_tokens, Google Ads API v23, Shopify GraphQL '2025-01', Next.js 14, localhost:3000, the ~15min intelligence-cache TTL, the advar- localStorage prefix, the platform type union 'google'|'meta'|'combined'. Cross-ref вҳ…DOC-OWNERSHIP-GUARD (the mechanical enforcer that would fail the build on the present-tense copies). src: 2026-07-17 CLAUDE.md audit. open [NP]

## I. LESSONS INDEX 1вҖ“60 (+ dated)  (source: LORAMER_DECISIONS.md)
1 Silent-skip via shared marker вҖ” use content-based idempotency, not marker-presence.
2 Scope assumption in destructure adds вҖ” grep the prop in the parent's scope before patching.
3 TS prop add = two edits/component (destructure AND type; check inline vs multi-line type).
4 JS string apostrophes break builds вҖ” use backticks for any string with apostrophes/quotes.
5 Stale anchors вҖ” re-read the current file (fresh sed/grep) before any patch.
6 Marker-collision silent failure вҖ” distinct sub-markers OR per-edit content checks.
7 Per-edit content-based idempotency check is the best practice (all/some/none present logic).
8 Silent .catch(()=>[]) hides GAQL/API errors вҖ” instrument console.error before concluding "no data".
9 Cache invalidation hides deployed fixes (15-min) вҖ” force a miss via a never-used date range.
10 Whitespace in anchors вҖ” bytes matter; dump exact bytes when an anchor fails.
11 PROMPT-AS-MIRROR вҖ” grounding/constraint text goes in code comments (INTERNAL_GROUNDING), never user-rendered prompt.
12 Meta breakdowns go in &breakdowns=, NOT &fields= (else HTTP 400, swallowed by .catch).
13 Same-line comment after a token (comma/paren/bracket/template) can break webpack вҖ” comment on its own line.
14 tsc --noEmit is NOT npm run build вҖ” webpack is stricter (syntax/mangled-literals); build is the real gate.
15 Surfacing raw API status/body into the prompt = diagnostic of last resort (always with a planned cleanup).
16 Anchor only from the current-turn paste вҖ” never memory/earlier turns/grep; small anchors over big.
17 Same-named files + blind mv is dangerous вҖ” unique-name downloads before moving.
18 Patch scripts with hardcoded machine paths silently fail вҖ” match the machine's path.
19 ONE canonical date resolver (resolveDateWindow) вҖ” never roll per-platform date math.
20 Revenue = NET (currentSubtotalPriceSet), not gross вҖ” surface refunds; match merchant analytics.
21 GAQL has NO LAST_90_DAYS enum вҖ” explicit BETWEEN via resolveDateWindow.
22 Platform selector and tab nav are separate controls вҖ” switch to Overview on platform change from a non-ad tab.
23 Safe Supabase dup cleanup вҖ” backupвҶ’repoint childrenвҶ’verify countsвҶ’delete only emptied twins (keeper isn't always older).
24 Bug hunts in big files вҖ” investigate-only first, then a tight fix spec.
25 Repo is single source of truth вҖ” git pull at session start on either machine; unpushed work doesn't travel.
26a Serverless backfill cross-request cursor race вҖ” do the whole job in ONE invocation (in-memory loop); persist the cursor only for resume-after-interrupt, never as the loop's control.
26b RightPanel renders TWIN desktop/mobile message containers (hidden md:flex / flex md:hidden, both in DOM) вҖ” audit BOTH when touching either; assign anchors by document order. (HANDOFF dual-numbered both as "26"; HANDOFF:730 explicitly notes the collision.)
27 zsh eats unquoted globs (quote --include="*.ts"); BSD grep needs -E for alternation.
28 Verify a freshly-deployed cron/route against LIVE prod + give it time (stale triggers/logs mislead).
29 Heredoc/terminal pastes drop characters вҖ” deliver code as files; tsc catches mangled identifiers, NOT mangled string literals вҖ” grep critical strings.
30 Backfill depth = "as deep as the platform serves," discovered by probing; report the ACTUAL earliest row, never the swept cursor.
31 Per-platform retention differs вҖ” probe before trusting any documented limit.
32 JSX comments are {/* */}, not /* */ (renders as visible text; tsc misses it).
33 CRON-GATED VERIFICATION вҖ” deploy before the cron window or manually trigger after; capture writes YESTERDAY's date.
34 Handoffs anchor on session TAG + files, never a commit hash (local commits squash/rewrite on push).
35 pg_dump in CI: invoke by ABSOLUTE path /usr/lib/postgresql/17/bin/pg_dump (PATH resolves to v16).
36 GitHub Actions "Re-run jobs" replays the ORIGINAL commit вҖ” use a fresh workflow_dispatch to test a fix.
37 Vercel env rotation needs a redeploy to bind; native cron rotates atomically with the redeploy.
38 Supabase DB password is reset-safe (app uses API keys, not raw Postgres password).
39 A DB write that must touch a row вҶ’ UPSERT (not UPDATE) + check affected count, log loudly on 0; never assume success on no-throw.
40 Never render internal flag/enum/status/tier keys to users вҖ” pass through a human-label map next to the keys.
41 Stripe Portal "cancel at period end" sets cancel_at (timestamp), not cancel_at_period_end (boolean).
42 Google OAuth consent-screen edits (name/domains/scopes/URLs/logo) trigger RE-verification вҖ” treat as frozen at launch.
43 Google Ads permissible-use update вҶ’ Tool Change Form (zero-risk MCC metadata), not a full Standard Access app.
44 Walk every onboarding identity SHAPE with a real identity before launch (founder-only testing only exercises one shape).
45 vercel env pull can report a populated prod var as blank вҖ” verify "empty env" against runtime behavior; never re-set to a guess.
46 An API probe verifies what the CREDENTIAL can see, not what EXISTS вҖ” a boundary coinciding with a known limit IS the explanation; scope-truncated $0 rows are false-zeros, delete them.
47 EVERYTHING GETS EVERYTHING вҖ” completeness is a CORRECTNESS requirement; every gap explicit; any cap is a logged deliberate decision (MATRIX).
48 Vercel MCP has NO env-write вҖ” rotate via CLI (value via stdin, never printed) + redeploy to bind.
49 Guard NOT-NULL numerics vs NaN at the WRITE BOUNDARY (Number.isFinite), not per-builder (NaN ?? 0 = NaN вҶ’ 23502 drops the whole row).
50 Don't conclude a logic bug from a symptom seen under one timing вҖ” replay the exact query against live DB; schedule catchup AFTER forward.
51 A backfill DRIVER LOOP must circuit-break on a persistent per-window error; never oscillate/re-walk; be gentle on live stores; resume from the TRUE frontier; when in doubt, STOP and surface.
52 Next.js App Router caches global fetch вҶ’ deterministic supabase-js reads/writes go STALE/DROPPED on Vercel; force-no-store on read-after-write routes; a unique request body masks the bug.
53 A persisted UI selection carried across a context switch must be RE-VALIDATED against the new context (derive caps from the incoming entity); land on a valid non-blank default.
54 Shopify managed-install scopes come from the DEPLOYED config (shopify app deploy), not the authorize-URL scope= param; a refresh preserves the original grant; verify a scope change by PROBE.
55 A flag-gated reconnect control can be invisible exactly when needed вҖ” any re-auth/extend-scope affordance must be reachable for a HEALTHY connection.
56 shopify app deploy needs the Shopify CLI on node вүҘ22.12 (CLI 4.x crashes on node 20).
57 Vercel env VALUES are unreadable from tooling (masked / pull-blanked / no MCP env tool) вҖ” confirm from the source system.
58 Shopify revenue basis differs BY GRAIN вҖ” reconcile to the cent (per-line refund attribution + pro-rata residual) or ship a silent per-SKU lie; a WRONG basis is worse than no basis.
59 A permanent-history backfill must self-reconcile per unit of work (ОЈ within 1Вў each day BEFORE write/cursor-advance) or HALT loudly вҖ” never persist a bad day.
60 A connection-state claim (broken/dead/frozen/blocked/unhealthy/reconnect-needed) is a HYPOTHESIS until a LIVE capture-path probe proves it вҖ” never written as fact from a stored flag (health/last_error_code/oauth_190/last_ok_at) alone; stored flags are DERIVED CONTEXT, not ground truth (same class as the Google end_date adapter-semantics bug). Origin: a prior session wrote "Influential Drones Meta BLOCKED/broken/oauth_190" into CONTINUE_HERE + QUEUE + a session log as settled fact from the flag alone вҖ” it was FALSE (token alive HTTP 200, warehouse reconciled to the penny) and survived days because each session read it forward without re-deriving. RULE: before writing any negative connection claim into ANY handoff doc, run a live probe (raw HTTP status + body, Lesson 15 style); until probed, record "flag says X вҖ” UNVERIFIED, probe before acting," never as a blocker. The transient-190-dark-flags-a-live-connection generator = WS2 #2 (separate fix).
61 A backfill writer must STOP AT its retention floor as an EMPTY SUCCESS (per-adapter granularMonths clamp вҖ” meta=36, GA fixed 2015-08-14, Google account/dim 132mo), NOT overshoot into a boundary THROW; a step is 'done' ONLY on empty-success-at-floor or reconciled-to-floor, NEVER on an error. Origin: the onboarding drain's Meta account step stoppedOnError at the ~37mo boundary (it overshot to 132mo), never completed, and BLOCKED the later placement step. Fix (LORAMER_ONBOARD_DRAIN_V1): granularMonths=36 for meta; PER-STEP-INDEPENDENT drain (a stuck early step never starves a later one); verified Meta taxonomy decides done-vs-retry-vs-surface ({1,2,4,17,613,80004}/429/timeout=retry В· 100В·1487534=narrow-the-window В· 100-other/190/368=surface В· empty-success=done); NEVER swallow the fetch error (L15) вҖ” surface code/subcode so floor-vs-transient is distinguishable.
62 A platform-wide "stall" + a cluster of serverless TIMEOUTS with NO DB/lock/deadlock evidence and NO code-deploy correlation = look UPSTREAM at the external API's QUOTA, not infra. The 2026-06-28 Google 504 cluster (06:20вҖ“11:40Z) AND the 4h geo "stall" were ONE event: Basic-Access developer-scope quota exhaustion (15k ops/day, one shared dev token) burned by the morning geo fan-out by ~11:32Z. FALSIFIED, explicitly: (a) Supabase swap/memory and (b) BUDGET_MS 680 вҖ” neither caused nor fixed the 504s (they ran 5.5h AFTER the BUDGET_MS deploy and stopped exactly when geo WRITES stopped, 3.5h BEFORE the Supabase resize). Read the REAL error bytes (e.errors[0]) before blaming infra; correlate the symptom's start/stop against the actual workload, not against whatever was deployed.
63 A backfill lap that throws OR fails to advance but lets the cron fire return HTTP 200 is a SILENT failure вҖ” geo was DEAD 4h under green 200s with the error masked as "[object Object]". Every drain fire must return ok:false/failed:N + console.error for ANY thrown/non-200 lap (ALL platforms); a dead/non-advancing lap can never read as a green fire. (LORAMER_GOOGLE_QUOTA_GUARD_V1 CHANGE 1.)
64 TWO completion authorities that can disagree are a stall trap: the sync_state cursor backfill_complete (writer) vs platform_connections.onboard_steps_done (drain). A stale done-flag over an INCOMPLETE cursor silently SKIPS a client forever (Woo Shelley: onboard ['woo'] done but cursor complete=false at 2018-12-13, owes to ~2015 вҖ” frozen ~12d; drain pending filter excludes her). The cursor must be the SINGLE completion authority; any path that re-opens a cursor to complete=false MUST clear that step key from onboard_steps_done.
65 Woo backfill "complete = one 21-day all-status-ZERO chunk" (woocommerce-backfill.ts) can FALSE-complete on any >21-day sales GAP mid-history вҖ” a quiet store stretch reads as history-start. When hardening woo completeness: probe the store's true oldest order, or require N consecutive zero chunks.
66 supabase-js .upsert(row) WITHOUT an explicit { onConflict } defaults its conflict target to the PRIMARY KEY. On a table whose real dedup key is a SECONDARY UNIQUE column (meta_tokens: PK=id + UNIQUE(user_email)), and where the PK is auto-generated (no id in the row), the upsert becomes an INSERT вҶ’ it violates the secondary UNIQUE вҶ’ 409, and if the returned error is discarded the write is a SILENT no-op that still looks successful. This bit the Meta callback: re-auth never rewrote the token (only the first-ever connect worked; the success redirect fired regardless), which broke the cote@ refresh. RULE: every upsert names its conflict target explicitly ({ onConflict: '<the-unique-column>' }) AND checks the returned error (fail loud вҖ” redirect/throw, never swallow, per L15). Gate-A a token/dedup upsert by reproducing the SECOND write to an existing key: buggy path 409s, fixed path UPDATES in place (id stable, 1 row). (LORAMER_META_CALLBACK_ONCONFLICT_V1, 2026-07-02.)
67 A Gate-A that checks only STATUS CODES can pass while the BEHAVIOR is broken вҖ” assert the behavior the gate exists to protect, not just 2xx/3xx. Origin: the 138a820 legacy-surface middleware silently broke the signup funnel two ways and that flight's Gate-A missed BOTH because it only read status codes: (a) it gated /agency + /business вҖ” the PRE-AUTH two-door signup pages вҖ” so unauthenticated new users were bounced to /login (the pages' content was never read вҶ’ public marketing doors misclassified as "legacy tenant pages"); (b) it redirected /dashboard вҶ’ -next BEFORE the /dashboard layout's enforceWelcomeGate could fire, so a fresh user reached the empty -next portfolio with NO account_type (Add-client 409s). The Gate-A even OBSERVED break (b) вҖ” /dashboard-next/clients returned 200 for a brand-new no-account_type user вҖ” and read it as "not over-blocked" instead of "onboarding didn't fire." RULE: for any gate/redirect/auth change, (1) READ what each matched path actually IS before gating it (public vs authed, data vs marketing), and (2) assert the POSITIVE behavior it must preserve вҖ” "a fresh user is REDIRECTED to /welcome", "the door RENDERS unauthenticated" вҖ” a bare 200 or 307 is necessary, NEVER sufficient. (LORAMER_SIGNUP_FUNNEL_FIX_V1, 2026-07-14.)
(2026-06-22) Product/line grain must reconcile to its account grain on the SAME revenue basis; re-capture history ONLY AFTER the basis fix ships (re-capturing before forces a second pass вҖ” violates "never twice").
